No. 1965/4 — MONDAY ,    MAY 02,  2016
EXTRAORDINARY
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
(Published by Authority)
PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government  Notifications
VIDESA  SEWA   PADAKKAMA
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the Commander
- in - chief of the Armed Forces has been graciously pleased to approve the awarding of the Videsa Seva Padakkama in terms
of regulation four of the proclamation instituting, constituting and creating the Videsa Seva Padakkama Published in the
Gazette Extraordinary, No.156/5 of 01st September 1981 to the persons named in the schedule hereto.
                                                                                          By His Excellency’s Command,
ENG . KARUNASENA HETTIARACHCHI,
Secretary,
Ministry of Defence.
Colombo,
04th April 2016.
VIDESA  SEV A  PADAKKAMA - 2015
